| <span data-ttu-id="443e0-958">Entrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="443e0-958">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="443e0-959">Value</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="443e0-959">Value</span></span> |
